        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer210432668" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12635922885845699304">Ok I'm giving this book 2 stars because by the end of the book I was so pissed off I could not stop shaking. I suppose that means that the author evoked the emotion she was looking for quiet well but it is not working for me.<br/><br/>*****Possible Spoilers Below*****<br/><br/>The bad guys just keep getting the upper hand over and over and over. If I met Calvin Malone as a real person I would not hesitate to gut him like a fish. His character reminds me of real people in the news and politics these days that just s</span>
  <span id="freeText12635922885845699304" style="display:none">Ok I'm giving this book 2 stars because by the end of the book I was so pissed off I could not stop shaking. I suppose that means that the author evoked the emotion she was looking for quiet well but it is not working for me.<br /><br />*****Possible Spoilers Below*****<br /><br />The bad guys just keep getting the upper hand over and over and over. If I met Calvin Malone as a real person I would not hesitate to gut him like a fish. His character reminds me of real people in the news and politics these days that just screw everyone over. And he gets away with it! The ass-backward thinking of the Pride Council has annoyed me through the series but I let it because not all species are the same and I respect that but now it's just getting ridiculous. Dealing with multiple deaths through-out this book was very difficult and only made the story that much more depressing.<br /><br />Faythe is learning that unless you have a penis and testicles that you will never really have power and that sucks. Even with you possess both pieces unless you're willing to crush everyone in your path you'll never hold onto power or be able to change anything. <br /><br />I did enjoy her testing of the waters with Jace and think it only right that she see that she can love more than one person but never really got the chance due to how she was raised. I really love her and Marc and hope to see them together in the end but Faythe deserves to follow her heart even if it ends up choosing Jace.<br /><br />It's exciting that Ethan's girlfriend is pregnant and what a miracle this represents for the Pride. I hope we get to see the birth and it's a girl! Wouldn't it be awesome to know that daughters were more likely with a mixed species baby?!?!?! It sure would take pressure off the tabbies and secure the population of the pride. I feel like there will be more to the story with this baby.<br /><br />I'm reading the last book now and am already pissed off with the direction of the story but I will hold out and hope/pray whatever that the author is setting it up for one hell of a HAE because if that isn't the case I'll be sadden to know I wasted 3 weeks reading a series that did nothing but disappoint me in the end.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12635922885845699304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_163596690" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/163596690" />
    <a title="Kim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2938528-kim"><img alt="Kim" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1300755705p2/2938528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/163596690?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim" href="/user/show/2938528-kim">Kim</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2938528-kim?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2938528-kim?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2938528-kim?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2938528-kim?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer163596690" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14082356306535523753">I had to force myself to go slowly with 'Shift'. After racing through the first 4 books, my body and mind couldn't handle another intense read straight away, and having spent so much time with Faythe and the gang I knew it was going to be an intense book. I'm glad 'Shift' didn't crush me emotionally as much as the previous books. There was certainly a lot of action and pain, both physically and emotionally, but I didn't find myself breaking as much as I have in the past. I was still affected by </span>
  <span id="freeText14082356306535523753" style="display:none">I had to force myself to go slowly with 'Shift'. After racing through the first 4 books, my body and mind couldn't handle another intense read straight away, and having spent so much time with Faythe and the gang I knew it was going to be an intense book. I'm glad 'Shift' didn't crush me emotionally as much as the previous books. There was certainly a lot of action and pain, both physically and emotionally, but I didn't find myself breaking as much as I have in the past. I was still affected by every word Rachel Vincent wrote and every problem Faythe had to face, but not to the point where I was falling to pieces. It was a welcome relief. <br /><br />I love how the addition of the thunderbirds changed the atmosphere of the series. While the Thunderbird problem was still set in werecat problems, there's something exciting about coming across a different speices of Shifters (sort of like when we met Kellar in 'Pride'). <br /><br />I felt so sorry for Kaci, she can't seem to escape being a possession, an asset to the most forceful enemy that can get their hands on her. I realise Faythe has come under similar attack in the past, but at least she's had more years and training to understand why the Prides act the way they do. <br /><br />I hate the conflict that is happening within the Prides, but mostly I hate Calvin Malone, because the actual fighting that happens keeps suspence going and the action described is half of what I love about this series. It's captivating and exciting and keeps me wanting more. I just hope they find a way to take Calvin down in 'Alpha'<br /><br />In terms of romance, while the problems were obviously going to cause trouble I wasn't as heartbroken by it. Shocked, of course, but not to the point of devestation like I thought I would be. As with all love triangles, you find yourself siding with one guy over the other, but the sad part is that bother guys are usually loveable and you never want to see them hurt. I hate that Faythe has to pick between them, but I can't help wanting her with the one I've fallen for. <br /><br />5/5 stars, can't wait to see how the series ends. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14082356306535523753" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_104329797" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/104329797" />
    <a title="Angela Corbett" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2617799-angela-corbett"><img alt="Angela Corbett" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1314316971p2/2617799.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/104329797?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela Corbett" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela Corbett" href="/user/show/2617799-angela-corbett">Angela Corbett</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer104329797&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer104329797" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18040888847803561404">I LOVE a good love triangle and Rachel Vincent has done such a great job with the triangle between Faythe, Jace and Marc! And the thing about the triangle is that I really didn't think it would happen. The hints about Jace having feelings for Faythe were always there, but Faythe and Marc were so committed to each other that I didn't expect a possible relationship between Jace and Faythe to ever be explored. I loved the interactions between the three of them in this book and enjoyed watching Fayt</span>
  <span id="freeText18040888847803561404" style="display:none">I LOVE a good love triangle and Rachel Vincent has done such a great job with the triangle between Faythe, Jace and Marc! And the thing about the triangle is that I really didn't think it would happen. The hints about Jace having feelings for Faythe were always there, but Faythe and Marc were so committed to each other that I didn't expect a possible relationship between Jace and Faythe to ever be explored. I loved the interactions between the three of them in this book and enjoyed watching Faythe grow and make decisions that are helping shape her into becoming a future Alpha. And I just love the boys. *sigh* I really don't know who I like more and I'm DYING to read the last book in the series. I keep telling myself it's only another 6 weeks to wait. <br /><br />I also love this series because Vincent isn't afraid to kill characters and knowing there are real consequences makes me even more invested in the story and the characters. I also love that Faythe is a strong, stubborn, independent heroine who won't be told what to do. I wish there were more books with characters just like her. I can't wait to see what happens next!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="18040888847803561404" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_115486851" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/115486851" />
    <a title="Sam Nicholas" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3398932-sam-nicholas"><img alt="Sam Nicholas" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1503237680p2/3398932.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/115486851?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sam Nicholas" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sam Nicholas" href="/user/show/3398932-sam-nicholas">Sam Nicholas</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer115486851" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9848264672316084419"> I had a hard time understanding this book and after the first chapter I was somewhat able to keep going on. I thought this was the first book in the series and as I was reading it I kept thinking 'If I wrote this book, this would not be the first.' So I went on goodreads and looked up the author Rachel Vincent and found out that this was the fifth book! I started laughing so hard, the library gave me the wrong book! I requested Stray and they gave me Shift. <br/> So once I got into the book and I wa</span>
  <span id="freeText9848264672316084419" style="display:none"> I had a hard time understanding this book and after the first chapter I was somewhat able to keep going on. I thought this was the first book in the series and as I was reading it I kept thinking 'If I wrote this book, this would not be the first.' So I went on goodreads and looked up the author Rachel Vincent and found out that this was the fifth book! I started laughing so hard, the library gave me the wrong book! I requested Stray and they gave me Shift. <br /> So once I got into the book and I was understanding what was happening I really liked it. This book was different than any other book out there. Most books are vampires and werewolfs but this one was werecats. I really liked the change no matter how small it was. This book was so good, honestly this series and the Mecedes Thompson novels are my personal favorites. They have so much in common. Now that I know that there are books before this one I am going to read those and maybe this book will make more sense! I really did like this book once I started to get it, and I suggest this book to anybody who loves fantasy fiction and needs a break from vampires and werewolfs!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9848264672316084419" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QtfV/NKWg/zXhrToIzRLnJYQ+/yRO3zo9iEPX/yufQDvCqSF7JMCPyOVWbJrdE67haDE3U2hOA16rKOF3IKD3w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('fSp9x+DE8m5xVC1JAzDoLYfQro0u0krCoUO4BBNJF3nQ9wy+3sFzrYVHwBNLcO0KlGCRrPJIDictzhTeM2Xppg==')})
  }
//]]>
